(a) **Shared (I5):** NEW `packages/shared/src/collection.ts`, exported from `index.ts`. `FieldTypeSchema` = 14 v1 types (text/longText/richTextLite/number/boolean/select/multiSelect/date/dateTime/image/file/json/relation/group). `CollectionField` is RECURSIVE (a `group` carries `fields` of sub-fields) ‚Äî modelled as `BaseFieldSchema` + lazy `SubFieldSchema`; `superRefine` enforces the v1 rules (select/multiSelect need `options`; relation needs `relation.collection`; group needs ‚â•1 sub-field and sub-fields may NOT be group/relation = one level deep; non-structural fields can't smuggle options/relation/fields). `CollectionSchema` = `{fields[‚â•1]}` + unique-key check + identifier-safe `key` regex. `CollectionDisplaySchema` (listColumns/defaultSort/titleField), `CollectionSlugSchema` (lower_snake_case). `RecordFilterSchema` (¬ß13.4): `where[]` of `{field, op‚ààeq|ne|gt|gte|lt|lte|contains|in|exists, value?}` (AND rows), `sort[]`, `limit‚â§1000`, `offset`. PURE `validateRecord(schema,input,{partial})` ‚Üí cleaned doc: coerces ("12"‚Üí12, "true"/"false"‚Üíbool), drops unknown keys, fills defaults, validates min/max/minLength/maxLength/regex/select-options/multiSelect-membership/date(ISO)/dateTime(parseable)/relation cardinality (one‚Üístring, many‚Üístring[])/group rows (array of objects, per-sub-field) ‚Äî collects `FieldError{path,message}` (dotted paths incl. `variants[0].stock`) and throws `RecordValidationError`; `partial` skips required-checks on absent keys (for PATCH-merge). `applyDefaults(schema,record)` = additive-safe read (ARCHITECTURE ¬ß13.3): fills newly-added field defaults, group/multiSelect/relation-many absent ‚Üí `[]`, scalar optional stays absent ‚Äî non-throwing, runs on every read. Helpers `indexedFields` (top-level, non-group, flagged), `labelText` (fa‚Üíen‚Üífallback). Definitions: `define` (dup-slug guard, syncs indexes), `updateDefinition` (bumps `version` on schema change, re-syncs indexes), `deleteDefinition` (drops indexes; records FK-cascade), `list`/`get`/`getBySlug`. Records: `insert`/`getRecord`/`update` (mode merge[default, shallow top-level merge then re-validate full doc]\|replace; `applyDefaults` on the current doc before merge so a newly-required-with-default field is filled = lazy migrate on write)/`deleteRecord`/`deleteWhere` (`MultiDeleteGuardError` unless `confirmMany`)/`count`/`find` (returns `{records, total}`; total ignores limit/offset). **Filter‚ÜíSQL compiler** (`compileWhere`/`compileOrder`): every clause is collection-scoped (`collection_id = ?`); field ‚Üí `json_extract(data,'$.'+sanitizeFieldPath(field))` where `sanitizeFieldPath` only allows `ident(.ident|[n])*` (throws on anything else ‚Üí no SQL injection via field names); values are ALWAYS bound params; `contains`‚Üí`LIKE ? ESCAPE '\\'` with `%_\\` escaped, `in`‚Üí`IN(?,‚Ä¶)` (empty‚Üí`0`), `exists`‚Üí`IS [NOT] NULL`, `ne`‚Üí`(x IS NULL OR x<>?)`, bool‚Üí0/1 (matches json_extract). **Computed indexes:** one SQLite EXPRESSION index per `indexed` field ‚Äî `CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS "recidx_<colid>_<key>" ON records (json_extract(data,'$.<key>')) WHERE collection_id='<colid>'`; `syncIndexes` creates wanted + drops stale on every define/updateDefinition; `dropIndexes` on delete; `indexNamesFor` exposed for tests. The `collections`/`records`/`files` tables + indexes already existed (migration 0001 from P3-T6 era) so NO new migration was needed. | 2026-06-13 | P3-T2 | `flow.loop` (batches) + `flow.merge` (append/wait-both/choose-first) with n8n-semantics contract tests (NODES.md ¬ßFlow, PLAN P3-T2). Registry now **17** types. **Architecture (two new NodeCtx capabilities, invariant I6 preserved ‚Äî the executor stamps them, the node never derives them):** (a) `ctx.nodeId` ‚Äî the executing node's graph id, so a STATEFUL node scopes its own `$vars` bucket and two instances of the same type never collide; (b) `ctx.inputsByPort: Record<port, FlowItem[]>` ‚Äî items grouped by the INPUT PORT they arrived on (empty ports filtered out, matching the router), so a branch-aware node can tell WHICH side fired (`execute()` still gets the flattened merge of all ports for the common case). `executor.ts#buildCtx` gained an `inputsByPort` param (set from `state.items`) and stamps both fields; harness `makeCtx` gained `nodeId`/`inputsByPort` overrides (defaults `node1`/`{}`). (b) **Shared (I5):** `FlowLoopParamsSchema` (`batch_size` z.coerce.int().min(1).default(1); `reset` bool default false); `FlowMergeParamsSchema` (`mode` enum append\\|wait_both\\|choose_first default append). (c) **Nodes:** `flow/loop.ts` ‚Äî n8n `splitInBatches`: ports `main`‚Üí`loop`+`done`; first entry stashes ALL items under `__loop__:<nodeId>` (`LOOP_STATE_PREFIX`) and emits the first batch on `loop`; each loop-back IGNORES the incoming (processed) items and emits the next slice, advancing the cursor; when batches run out it clears state and emits ALL originals on `done`; empty input ‚Üí straight to `done` with []; `reset` discards leftover state. `flow/merge.ts` ‚Äî ports `input1`+`input2`‚Üí`main`; reads `ctx.inputsByPort` exclusively (the flattened `items` arg is intentionally unused): `append` passes each branch straight through (input1 first if both present, no waiting/state); `wait_both` buffers the first side under `__merge__:<nodeId>` (`MERGE_STATE_PREFIX`) and emits NOTHING until the other arrives, then emits both together (input1 first) and clears; one-sided ‚Üí never emits; `choose_first` emits the first branch and latches (`{fired:true}`) so later activations are no-ops. Both registered in `builtinNodes` (15‚Üí17); `flow-data-nodes.test.ts` count assertion relaxed to `>=13` (authoritative exact count now lives in the newest phase's test). (d) **Editor:** fa/en keys `nodes.flow.{loop,merge}.label`, `nodeDesc.flow.{loop,merge}`, `param.{batch_size,reset}`, `option.mode.{append,wait_both,choose_first}` (parity compile-enforced); both nodes auto-appear in the palette via GET /api/node-types. | 2026-06-13 | P3-T1 | **Phase 3 started** ‚Äî `flow.executeSubFlow` + `flow.return` (reusable sub-flows; NODES.md ¬ß"Execute Sub-Flow", ARCH ¬ß10). Registry now **15** types. Architecture: a node never runs an executor itself (invariant I6) ‚Äî the host injects a new `ctx.subflow` capability, mirroring the `ctx.code.run` precedent.
